 com / fxhogubmox After the demonetisation, the picture that was seen outside banks and atms has definitely changed
 lekin log ab bhi pareshaani se jujh rahe hai
 In the past, people had the most trouble while withdrawing their own money and depositing it in the bank
 isaki ek badi vajah jo nikal kar saamne ai he voexenjakaraane aa rahe logon kii badi sankhya kii thi
 So when the exchange was banned at banks' counters, it also made the lines shorter
 bainkon ke baahar lagane vaali lambii kataron ko kam karne ke liye arabiai or centre sarkaar ne kai baar paise ke lenden ke niyamon main badlaav kiya
 Guidelines were made several times and changes were made several times, but the problem remained the same
 line choti-badi hoti rahi hai, lekin mul sawaal logon ko apane paise ko lekar ho rahi pareshaani kaa he
 The question arising on demonetisation is not BJP, worrying for Modi
 After the closure of the exchange, the team till date visited the lines outside many banks
 is dauraan sabase ahm baat yah saamne ai ki log piem ke faisle or exange band karne niyam se to khush dikhe, lekin abhi bhi len-dein main lag rahe vakt se pareshaan dikhe
 One of the problems of the people is that they are not getting the money from the bank as per their need
 bainkon se paisa nikaalane kii limit sarkaar ne tay kii hui he, lekin kai log aise hai, jinhen jaruri kaamon ke liye zyada paise chahie
 After withdrawing cash at a time, people are unable to muster the courage to get in line again the next day or next week
 lihaaja log in niyamon main bhi dheel kii maang kar rahe hai
 Tribals living a life of ease away from the noise of demonetisation
 First of all, when we talk about the people engaged in the line in the bank branch, the biggest problem here is about time
 bainkon main kaamkaaj kii gati ko lekar logon me naaraazgi dikhi

 isse logon kii naaraazgi or badhati he

 With the help of special equipment installed in these shoes, the family and friends of the patient can monitor them from far away and this will give a little more freedom to the patients as well
 sutron ke anusaar, britain main aise juute 250 pound main bik rahe hai

 saamaanya juuton kii tarah hi dikhne vaale is juute kii hill main jeepies (global pojishning system) lagaaya gaya he
 This device cannot be seen or felt
 hill main lage is upkaran main ek bydaree, ek sim card (jo lokation jaanane main madad karata he) or ek isi lagi hui he jo upkaran ko kaam karne main madad karti he

 aam taur par baishakh kaa maheenaa april may main shuru hota he
 It is called Vaishakh due to its relation with the Visakha nakshatra
 is maheene main dhan prapti or punya prapti ke tamaam avasar aate hai
 Lord Vishnu, Parashurama and Devi are worshiped mainly in this month
 varsh main keval ek baar shri banke bihari ji ke charan darshan bhi isi maheene main hote hai
 In this month, Ganga or lake bath is of special importance
 aam taur par isi samay se lok jivan main mangal kaary shuru hote hai
 This time the month of Vaishakh will be from April 20 to May 18
 baishakh main daan karne kaa mahatv-baishakh ko fal prapti kaa maheenaa kaha jaataa he
 Donation is more important in the month of Vaishakh
 kaha jaataa he ki is maheene daan karne se garibi dur hoti he
 One should bathe in the holy rivers in this month
 manyata he ki baishakh ke maheene main puja aradhana kar ke jivan kii samasyaon se mukti pai ja sakati he
 Which are the main fasts and festivals of Vaishakh month? - In this month, Ganga is worshiped on the tenth day of Shukla Paksha
 - isi maheene main bhagwaan buddha or parashuram kaa janm bhi hua tha
 In this month, Lord Brahma created sesame seeds, so there is special use of sesame seeds
 - isi maheene main dhan or sampatti prapti kaa mahaparv akshay tritiya bhi aata he
 - In this month comes Mohini Ekadashi, which can be special blessing of Shri Hari
 baishakh maheene main khan paan kaa kya khyaal rakhen?- is maheene main garmi kii maatra lagaataar teevr hoti jaati he
 Therefore, the risk of all types of communicable diseases increases
 - is maheene main jal kaa prayog badha dena chahie or tel vaali chize kam se kam khaani chahie
